Your Moon Sign

In order to find your Moon sign, look for the two entries that are exactly before and after your date of birth.
Source: The American Ephemeris for the 20th/21st Century by Neil F. Michelsen

Example: on January 2nd, 1900, at 21:26 London time, the Moon enters Aquarius, and stays there untill January 4th at 22:09, when it enters Pisces.
